Create Table dbo.[AchievedTable] ( [ID] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1),
[MemberCode] varchar (200)  NULL ,
[SponsorCode] varchar (200)  NULL ,
[DateOfAchievement] varchar (200)  NULL ,
[WeekNumber] varchar (200)  NULL ,
[Status] varchar (200)  NULL ,
[RewardName] varchar (200)  NULL ,
[Level] int  DEFAULT ((0)) NULL ,
[AutoDateInsert] datetime  DEFAULT (getdate()) NULL ,
[idate] int  DEFAULT ((0)) NULL ,
[ClosingNumber] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[PaidDate] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Rank] varchar (500)  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[ActivatedMemberList] ( [ID] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[MemberCode] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[PrevEPin] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[NewEPin] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[ActivationDate] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Activation_iDate] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[AutoInsertDateTime] datetime  DEFAULT (getdate()) NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[Admin_login] ( [id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[User_id] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Pwd] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Type] varchar (5000)  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[binary_status] ( [name] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[member_code] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[introducer_code] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[left_child] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[right_child] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[people_no] varchar (500)  DEFAULT ((0)) NULL ,
[filled] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[BV] float  DEFAULT ((0)) NULL ,
[countChild] int  DEFAULT ((0)) NULL ,
[Level] int  DEFAULT ((0)) NULL ,
[middle_child] varchar (100)  DEFAULT ('') NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[BV_valuue] ( [id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[Product_type] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Product_id] varchar (500)  NULL ,

Create Table dbo.[Member_topup_details] ( [id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[Member_code] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Packageid] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Package_amount] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Package_pv] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Entry_Date] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Entry_TIme] varchar (500)  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[Member_Upgrade_History] ( [Id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[Member_code] nvarchar (500)  NULL ,
[Sponcer_code] nvarchar (500)  NULL ,
[Upgrade_date] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Upgrade_idate] int  NULL ,
[Upgrade_time] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Upgrade_Pin] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Upgrade_Packageid] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Upgrade_amt] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[PV] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Pay_Status] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Pay_Istatus] int  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[MemberPairLevel] ( [ID] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[MemberCode] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[PairAchieved] int  NULL ,
[IsUsed] int  DEFAULT ('0') NULL ,
[AchievedDate] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[AutoInsertDateTime] datetime  DEFAULT (getdate()) NULL ,
[ClosingNumber] varchar (500)  DEFAULT ((0)) NULL ,
[Interval] varchar (500)  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[Message_allocation_details] ( [Message_allocated] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Message_reminder] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Message_used] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[ID] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY   );

Create Table dbo.[Message_config] ( [Id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[uid] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[sender] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[route] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[domain] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Status] varchar (500)  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[message_corner] ( [Sender_id] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Sender_name] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Receiver_id] varchar (5000) NOT NULL ,
[Receiver_name] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Subject] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Message] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Date] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY   );

Create Table dbo.[Message_send_details] ( [ID] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,

[Status] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Time] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[messageurl] nvarchar (MAX)  NULL ,
[resulturl] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Type] varchar (500)  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[NewsTable] ( [Heading] varchar (50)  NULL ,
[News] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Date] varchar (50)  NULL ,
[id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[filepath] varchar (500)  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[oedered_product_product_wise] ( [order_no] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[product_code] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[product_name] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[category] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[MRP] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[discount] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[CP] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[quantity] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[total] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[date] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[user_code] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Product_status] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Product_paymentstatus] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Time] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Idate] int  NULL ,
[id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[product_user] varchar (5000)  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[ordered_product_bill_wise] ( [order_no] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[user_code] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[user_name] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[total_amount] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[date_of_purchase] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[mobile_no] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[shipping_date] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[delivery_date] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[shipping_address] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[status] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[Payment_status] varchar (5000)  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[OrderShippingAddress] ( [Id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[order_no] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[userid] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[name] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[company] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[address] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[city] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[country] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[state] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[postalcode] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[mobile] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[date] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[idate] int  NULL ,
[District] varchar (5000)  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[Package_details] ( [id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[Packageid] int  NULL ,
[Product_id] int  NULL ,
[Date] varchar (5000)  NULL ,

Create Table dbo.[Stock_Point_Deatils] ( [Id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[Stock_Point_Code] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Stock_Point_Name] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Mobile_No] varchar (50)  NULL ,
[Address] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[User_id] varchar (50)  NULL ,
[Password] varchar (50)  NULL ,
[Date] varchar (50)  NULL ,
[Idate] int  NULL ,
[Time] varchar (50)  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[SubCategory_details] ( [category_id] varchar (8000)  NULL ,
[sub_category_name] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[sub_category_id] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[sub_cato_icon] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY   );

Create Table dbo.[subscribed_email] ( [Id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[Email_id] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Date] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Idate] int  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[top_achiver_details_list] ( [member_code] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[member_name] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[achiever_pin] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[date] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[member_imagepath] varchar (5000)  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[TopUpMemberList] ( [ID] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[MemberCode] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[PrevEPin] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[NewEPin] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[ActivationDate] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Activation_iDate] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[AutoInsertDateTime] datetime  DEFAULT (getdate()) NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[Training_schedule] ( [Id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[Membercode] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Heading] nvarchar (MAX)  NULL ,
[Training_Details] nvarchar (MAX)  NULL ,
[Location] nvarchar (MAX)  NULL ,
[Date] varchar (50)  NULL ,
[Idate] int  NULL ,
[Time] varchar (50)  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[Transfer_epin_member] ( [Memberid] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Member_name] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Transfer_to] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Transferto_name] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Transfer_date] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Epin] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[ID] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY   );

Create Table dbo.[TrioAchieveAmount] ( [ID] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1),
[MemberCode] nvarchar (50)  NULL ,
[LeftAmount] float  DEFAULT ((0)) NULL ,
[RightAmount] float  DEFAULT ((0)) NULL ,
[IsUsed] int  DEFAULT ((0)) NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[TrioAmount] ( [ID] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[MemberCode] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[LeftAmount] float  NULL ,
[RightAmount] float  NULL ,
[Date] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[MemberBy] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[InsertAutoDateTime] datetime  DEFAULT (getdate()) NULL ,
[IsUsed] int  DEFAULT ((0)) NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[twoistoonetable] ( [Membercode] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Date] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[ID] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[Deleteid] int  NULL ,
[Closingno] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Idate] int  NULL ,
[interval] varchar (500)  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[Update_bank_payment] ( [Id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[Member_code] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Bankname] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Transaction_id] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Amount] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Slippath] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Date] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Idate] int  NULL ,
[Time] varchar (50)  NULL ,
[IFSCCode] varchar (100)  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[User_registration] ( [Id] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[Usercode] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Email_id] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Name] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Password] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Mobile_no] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Status] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Date] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Idate] int  NULL ,
[address] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[nearest_location] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[city] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[state] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[district] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[pin] varchar (5000)  NULL   );

Create Table dbo.[Virtual_payout] ( [Membercode] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Date] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Payout] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[Time] varchar (5000)  NULL ,
[ID] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY   );

Create Table dbo.[WebsiteMessage] ( [ID] int NOT NULL  IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY ,
[FirstName] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[LastName] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[EmailID] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[Message] varchar (MAX)  NULL ,
[Date] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[iDate] varchar (500)  NULL ,
[AutoInserDateTime] datetime  DEFAULT (getdate()) NULL   );
